	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#a59da9>大石</color>", NULL, "<color=#a59da9>Ooishi</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 11, "ps3/s14/11/220700252", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「鞄…？",
			NULL, "\"A bag...?", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 11, "ps3/s14/11/220700253", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　そりゃ、どんなやつですか？」",
			NULL, " What's inside?\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//窓口警官rvS14/00/centA11007.「一応、確認しましたけどね。kvS14/00/centA11008.どうやらカメラと、フィルムの類ですね…。kvS14/00/centA11009.どうしましょうか？」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#f5e6d3>窓口警官</color>", NULL, "<color=#f5e6d3>Attendant Policeman</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 0, "ps3/s14/00/centa11007", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「一応、確認しましたけどね。",
			NULL, "\"I checked it earlier.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 0, "ps3/s14/00/centa11008", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "どうやらカメラと、フィルムの類ですね…。",
			NULL, " There's apparently a camera and some kind of film.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 0, "ps3/s14/00/centa11009", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "どうしましょうか？」",
			NULL, " What should we do about it?\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 3000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 1300, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	DrawBustshot(6, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene( "black", 3000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

}
